< text>
This was my first time going here but I will definitely be going back. When we arrived (party of two) we were greeted by staff with a Hi and a friendly smile and told to take a seat wherever we liked.
It took less then 10 minutes for staff to come to our table and ask if we wanted any drinks, we ordered and she left. When she returned, we ordered our food. This consisted of one dish each and a plate of rice that we would share.
Now this is where they lost a star! It took over 30 minutes to get our food and although it was still warm and very tasty, that was just way to long. Also the staff didn't come to the tables and say, sorry for the wait or offer us a second glass of Soda or Water!
Nevertheless the food was great!üòã So go check them out and don't miss out on a great food find!üòä<//text>

< text>
This place is pretty average.  If you know what to order, the meals will be decent (pad se ew, papaya salad and tom yum).  If you venture out of your nomral order like the Orange Chicken, you'll will be dissapointed.  It is the driest and most bland orange chicken you'll ever encounter.  Panda express is far superior to the ones here.  Another dissapointment are their pho, curries and bbq. It is Merced and you shouldn't expect it to compare to LA or Bay Area.<//text>

< review>
It is very popular and by extension very busy. Expect to wait sometime before you are seated as this place gets pretty crowded at times. I've gone in for just an order of pad thai without calling ahead, (rookie mistake), and waited upwards of 20 minutes after ordering. I also ordered a thai ice tea, which was about the size of a typical small drink, for $5. It is a bit pricey so if you are looking for a place that is cheap or you just want to get a quick bite this is probably not the place to go. But I must say that the ambience inside is very pleasant. So if you're looking for a nice night out with friends and don't mind paying a little extra this is the place to go. The food was exceptional and I highly recommend you try it at least once.</review>

104636687373132435944<//user_id>
< text>
This is my go-to tire shop.  I went in to VItness to get one of my tires checked out - it had a screw in it.

Once I parked in the garage, the owner came out to inquire about the service I needed.  I told him about the screw in the tire and he said that because the screw was on the side of the tire, there was nothing that could be done to repair it.

FYI- if you get a screw/nail in your tire, that tire is reparable only if it is on the thread (middle of the tire).  If it is on the side, it is not reparable and a new tire is needed.

I verified this information using my smart phone - hey you never know...I certainly didn't.

The guy said he'd pull it out with the hope that just on the surface and hence no replacement would be needed.  Alas, that was not the case, as when he started pulling the screw out, the tire started deflating.

The unfortunate thing is I had just replaced my tires no more than a year ago - still lots of miles to go.

The entire replacement of my tire was $85 including tax.  Overall, the service was done professionally and quickly.  I was in/out in 20 minutes.< /text>

<review>HIDDEN GEM IN MARIN.

I went in Monday, and they had their new Gravity Prime Rib menu... WOW!!

This is my 3rd time going to Gravity, the atmosphere there is great. Lighting is low, as well as ambient sound (even when full) making it easy to maintain a good and enjoyable conversation with whoever you are with. Staff is very friendly and knowledgeable from what I have experience.

Food prices are good for food that is local and organic; and the seafood is caught the same day from what I was told.

The Prime Rib Monday is a great deal.

You get a 3-course meal.
A salad, a 12oz  prime rib with baked potato (it was delicious), and a pudding at the end that you will love even if you thought you weren't a pudding type of person (true story ;) )

They serve some type of made in house bread and butter.
Totally worth it for $35, i would definitely recommend gravity to anyone looking for great quality food and cocktails, oh and its family owned.

<rating>5< /rating>< Text>
Picked up my dress today and I'm so happy with it!! Not gonna lie, I was worried since this is the first custom anything I've ever done. The team has been a pleasure to work with, very accommodating and strive their best to achieve customer satisfaction. And I am completely satisfied! They've kept me updated via email throughout the entire process and always asked me for input on specific design decisions (like special lace and beading). Luckily, today was my first fitting and it fit PERFECTLY! I was nervous because of the change my body went through since I first came in for my measurements, but my dress is beautiful and comfortable! Needless to say, I didn't need any major alterations. Lucky, lucky, me!

At times I did feel unsure of my initial decisions, but they always had input and recommendations to make my vision come to life. I can't tell you enough how happy I am with the turnout (and turn around time). IMO, it's a great price for the customization - when you think about it, the dress is made to YOUR measurements and YOUR proportions. They aren't cutting off detail at the bottom like most "off the rack" places, because they make it to fit you! They know what they're doing, and even ask ahead of time how all you think your heels will be to make the length of the dress just perfect. On your first visit, just bring in pictures of all the dresses you love and are inspired by and they will work with you. Trust the process!! I will say though that there were times where I was unsure of their recommendations (because I don't have that designer eye and it's hard to envision everything coming together when you're nervous about a custom order). But the finished product will leave you feeling elated! Thank you team, you ladies are the best! I'll post pictures after the big day!<//Text>

This is a gluten free review.

Gluten free menu: No, but GF items clearly marked

Gluten free options: 5/5
Pretty much the entire menu is gluten free. I really appreciate that they itemize all major allergens for every item on their menu.

I do plan on asking if their falafels are actually gluten free but maybe just fried in a shared fryer. If they are gluten free then I look forward to trying them the next time around.

Food: 2/5
Portions are good for one person. Everything tasted fresh and very healthy, but kind of bland. Also, I'm a white meat chicken eater and just wasn't a fan of the meat quality. I had quite a bit of dark meat and some cartilage in my bowl, which was pretty unappetizing.

Service: 4/5
Staff was friendly and helpful at explaining how to order and what they would recommend combining in the bowl (especially sauces...there's so many options).

Location: 4/5
Super easy to park and find the restaurant

Ambiance: 3/5
Comfortable. Nothing special. Feels like any other fast food restaurant setting.

Price: 3/5
About $15 per person with a drink

Overall score: 3/5

I'll come back and give Cava one more try. Hope its a better experience the second time around.< /Text>

< Text>
The food taste good but the portions are a bit off. They hardly provide any meat, we're talking 2 small meatballs if you order half meatballs. And when you order a grains and greens bowl, they put like a half a spoon of rice, its like a bad joke. The bill ends up being like $14 just for a bowl of food, and if you don't top it with all of the extras, you'll be very disappointed in how little meat and rice actually comes with the bowl. Since you are forced to top the bowl with some extras so that you can actually feel satisfied with your meal, by the time you eat, all the meat is cold as the temperatures have mixed.

All around, I will not be coming back to CAVA due to the expensive price for a not-so-satisfying meal.< /Text>

<Date>1485873792208</Date><gmapID>0x80dcdc34352478d7:0x20017cf4f2a12ff8< /gmapID><Review>I love this place! A Paleo friendly, quick Chipotle style service, low prices and convenient. It can't be topped. I had this in Washington DC and wished it was in California and now we have it! I love it. There are many great savory and spicy options which keep it fresh and new every visit.

Your base: has 8 options, lentils, white rice, brown rice, arugula, romaine, baby spinach,  super greens mix, mesclun mix. There's no place that has as many quality leafy green options to choose from. They allow you to mix and match. My favorite is the super greens with kale brussel sprouts, broccoli, chicory, and cabbage.

The dips: They give you 3 sides to choose from out of 6 options: Hummus , a roasted red pepper hummus , tzaziki, eggplant and red pepper, crazy feta, harrisa. In my opinion, all the options taste good. When I say they taste good, I don't mean ok. Compared to other foods of this kind, they excel.

Meat: Choose 1 from 6 options. They do have a veggie option for vegetarians. I tried the lamb meat balls and chicken. Both tasted great. The meat balls were a little dry, but that's not uncommon with this style. They offer: veggies, chicken, lamb meatballs, beef, shredded lamb (very juicy) , and beef meatballs.

Dressing/Topping: I believe they have six options. I don't remember the names of any of them. I tried two and both were great tasting.

Bonus: They have pleasant service here. Washington DC isn't known for its service where this chain has many of its locations.<//Review><name>Charlton Bilow< /name><pictures>None<//pictures><Rating>5<//Rating></record>
